commit 0fa23bd0fc1ea9b25474699fc22495c2ba4eea24
Author: Shish <shish@shishnet.org>

    Add (Karaoke Ver) to 'vocaltrack=off' tracks in the printed track list
    
    >90% of tracks have vocals - instead of having a whole column for
    "vocaltrack on/off", we can get rid of that column and just specially
    mark the few who don't fit.
    
    Previously:
    
    ```
    Track          Vocal
    A              On
    B              On
    C              On
    D              Off
    E              On
    F              On
    G              On
    ```
    
    With this patch:
    
    ```
    Track
    A
    B
    C
    D (Karaoke Ver)
    E
    F
    G
    ```

commit 6f453046033e152e408619817f76589d3636a92d
Author: Shish <shish@shishnet.org>
Date:   2018-08-03 12:40:29 +0100

    No need to send session key inside the websocket connection
    
    The server will now look at the HTTP headers
    
    Aside from the general niceness of avoiding duplicate work, this is also
    necessary for local development of the player -- when the .html file is
    opened from file://, it doesn't have permission to view the cookies of
    http://localhost/, so the cookie-parsing regex will fail. But if we go
    ahead and create a connection from file:// to http://localhost, the web
    browser will add the correct cookies even though we can't see them for
    ourselves.

0	5	player2/src/player.js
6	1	website/karakara/__init__.py

commit 41a4da866320872100dda4f666b3972979fde630
Author: Richard Lancaster <richard@rl0.co.uk>
Date:   2015-01-20 21:18:32 +0000

    Probe the fps of the source video and specify for final video
    
    This fixes an issue with videos with that declare
    a variable frame rate but actually aren't (a
    surprising amount!?), mencoder would use the
    maximum rate, meaning the video in the final
    video would end before the music had finished.
    
    This will not work for videos that have truely
    variable frame rates. As far as I know, mencoder
    doesn't support these.
    
    Useful environment variable that drops you into
    a shell if the program end unexpectedly.
